lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许传梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生。家住青岛市北区武宁路</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">号</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">306</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">户。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初，许传梅来到山东日照市莒县姐姐家，姐妹俩外出讲法轮功真相，被当地派出所警察抓捕，许传梅被劫持到济南山东省第一女子劳教所劳教一年。期间许传梅被关小黑屋，不让大小便，不让洗澡。因为拒不配合邪恶，被野蛮灌食，嘴角被撕伤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，许传梅在青岛市北区嘉豪市场发放法轮功资料，被开平路派出所警察抓捕，被到关押青岛普东看守所，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被青岛市北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许传香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东日照市莒县乔山镇郝家洪沟法轮功学员。许传香<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在招贤镇招贤大街张贴法轮功真相资料时，被招贤镇派出所警察抓捕。警察抄家，抢走<span lang="EN-US">3</span>本大法书籍、计算机主机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台、笔记本计算机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台，扣押踏板摩托车<span lang="EN-US">1</span>辆，并将许传香关押到莒县拘留所拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月份将从日照看守所转往济南山东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许凤梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南周口市东新区法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。家住周口市东新区许湾乡许湾村。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年遭劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被警察入室抓捕、抢劫，关押到周口看守所。接着，邪党公、检、法人员又构陷罪名，将其判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许高瑞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府法轮功学员许章清涂爱莲之子。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。许高瑞刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许光利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年出生，湖北荆门市人，向往并推崇自由民主普世价值。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底因涉嫌颠覆国家政权被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，被当局构陷与别人合谋炸毛泽东故居以涉嫌犯放火罪，爆炸罪判处有期徒刑一年八个月。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日圣诞节刑满释放。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日到沈阳祭奠病逝在沈阳医院的诺贝尔和平奖得主刘晓波，被沈阳当局关押将近四十个小时，手机被破坏无法使用。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日屠夫吴淦开庭，恰逢许光利去天津旅游，落地天津便被天津当局抓捕，被关押十余个小时后才被释放。许光利<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日购买了广东清远开往湖北衡阳的车票，其后就失去联系。后获悉被荆门警方刑事拘留。而<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日家属得到批捕通知书，批捕罪名是涉嫌寻衅滋事罪。一审法院于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日向其送达一审判决书，许光利获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许红卫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省烟台市蓬莱市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，许红卫被山东省蓬莱市法院非法判决<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午，山东省蓬莱市法轮功学员许红卫在家门口，被蓬莱市国保便衣带走，当日下午蓬莱国保又进行抄家。被关押在蓬莱看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，许红卫被蓬莱市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日许红卫案开庭。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。许红卫在<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月曾因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，曾遭酷刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许来福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：许来福被判</span>有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">许丽华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省榆树市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年七十三岁。二零一一年，许丽华曾被判刑三年，一直在吉林省女子监狱遭迫害三年。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">许丽华在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月疫情期间，在大街上贴法轮功传单，被人诬陷，遭华昌派出所警察抓捕、后“取保候审”。华昌派出所警察仍在继续构陷许丽华老太至德惠市检察院和法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，许丽华老太被德惠市法院判刑三年，已被押入吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许那（又名许娜）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，当年天安门广场上的绝食学生中，有一位名叫许那（又名许娜），是北京广播学院（现中国传媒大学）的学生。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年前，她曾和同学高举“新闻自由，言论自由”的横幅，满怀希望地走在北京街头游行的人群中。<span lang="EN-US">32</span>年后，许那仍在北京，却已在东城区看守所被刑事羁押了一年多时间。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，许那和于宙在参加一场同道聚会后双双被拘留四十多天。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，许那因为外地来京的法轮功朋友提供住宿而再次被捕，后被判五年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年初，随着奥运会的临近，各地异议人士遭到抓捕，包括法轮功修炼者。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚上，于宙、许那在演唱会结束后开车回家的路上，被警方拦住搜查。警察在其车中搜出一本法轮功书籍，将夫妇二人带到通州拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天后正值除夕，体格健壮的于宙突然离奇死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁。当局声称于宙死于绝食或糖尿病。悲痛欲绝的许那被判处三年有期徒刑。于宙的真实死因至今成谜。于宙、许那的案件见于国际特赦<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月向联合国普遍定期审议递交的报告、美国“国会及行政当局中国委员会”的分析报告、美国国际宗教自由委员会<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度报告。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，许那第三次被捕。当天<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括许那在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。许那等人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，许那被北京当局宣判，获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/8.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/8.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，辽宁抚顺市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，许秀云到李石寨发法轮功真相资料，被警察抓捕，许秀云被关入戒毒所。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，许秀云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，许秀云被关押到辽宁女子监狱，遭受惨无人道的酷刑折磨：<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午两点左右，许秀云在西一路交通岗附近给路人免费发送翻墙卡，被两个便衣抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被抚顺市东洲法院开庭，法官田浩以许秀云曾冤狱十三年、出狱未出五年为借口，诬陷其「累犯」，再重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">许章清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北孝感市孝南区新铺镇政府公务员，法轮功学员。每天早出晚归，工作兢兢业业几十年。妻子涂爱莲，是孝南区新铺镇远大小学退休教师，退休才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，在家帮忙带孙女。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚许章清、涂爱莲夫妇、许章清的儿子许高瑞遭警方抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。湖北孝感市下辖安陆市法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下达对许章清<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人的判决：许章清被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，妻子涂爱莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，他们未修炼法轮功的儿子许高瑞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；同时每人还被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。许章清刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许志永：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，河南省商丘市民权县人，前北京邮电学院专业讲师，前北京市海淀区人民法院人民陪审员，“公盟”重要创始人，青年法学家、宪政学者和公民维权代理人，就全国人大对《城市流浪乞讨人员收容遣送办法》进行违宪审查提议者，新公民运动倡导者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被北京市警方以涉嫌“聚扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘，关押在北京市第三看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，刑满获释；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被广州市警方从番禺海鸥岛杨斌律师处带走；据悉，其此次被抓，疑与<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月曾因参加“厦门聚会案”遭通缉有关，许志永自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日丁家喜律师被捕后就一直在中国南方秘密流亡。其亲友均遭多次骚扰跟踪，其女友李翘楚亦被强迫失踪，后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被以涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师接到临沂市检察院电话：丁、许二案均第二次退回公安补充侦查。许志永现羁押于山东省临沭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">薛莲霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛市黄岛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，黄岛区西海岸（原胶南）薛莲霞在大珠山某小区发真相资料时，被一青年人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，薛莲霞被黄岛区大珠山派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，薛莲霞被取保候审，女儿去派出所交了<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元保证金。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午，薛连霞被胁迫去了法院就没回来。她家人听人说，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span minor-latin;">于桂兰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于海勇</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、于健莉、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于娇茹</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于雷</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于向家</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于云峰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余德贞、余凤连、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余光河、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余慧明</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、余江帆、余浚聪、余荣新、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">余绍萍、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">玉杰（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁王柱、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁玉芹、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">袁志强、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岳长友</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">牙里坤<span lang="EN-US">.</span>肉孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">Yalqun Rozi</span>，维吾尔族知名作家、讲师和学者，原新疆教育出版社高级编辑，中国在押政治犯。作为高级知识分子，因其长期花费精力编辑了一大批维吾尔人文教科书，发表过若干有关维吾尔文化文章，并于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年帮助编写了中小学校维吾尔教学大纲和语文教学课程，随颇受社会广泛欢迎，并成为维吾尔知识分子中的典范；但自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月陈全国被任命为新疆党委书记起，因其极左思想将从事维吾尔教科书的工作均视为“意识形态问题的表现”，故而其及众多同行遂遭严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其及其所属教科书编辑公司的全体成员突遭乌鲁木齐市警方抓捕，因抓捕之初并未受到指控，故其涉嫌罪名不详，但自此失联；据悉，因其自被捕至判刑以来，一直无具体信息，故而其身体健康状况及所押地点等均不知情；其家属请求探视、通信权等亦遭拒绝。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，知其被中共新疆当局以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">闫卫宾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，河南省驻马店市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，在宣讲法轮功的过程当中被诬告，当天下午，驻马店市老街派出所警察到其家中抄家，抄出闫卫宾写的诉江信件等物品；并将闫卫宾抓捕到老街派出所，后被刑事拘留。在被关押期间，派出所人员再次返回闫卫宾家中又进行了抄家，并抄出<span lang="EN-US">1</span>千份法轮功传单。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，闫卫宾被批捕，后被关押到驻马店市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份时，已被构陷到驿城区法院。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，闫卫宾在驻马店市驿城区法院被秘密开庭。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份又进行了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日闫卫宾的家人接到驿城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">闫喜华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省双鸭山市退休女教师，法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬，闫喜华老人在双鸭山集贤县发放法轮功资料时，被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被双鸭山市尖山法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前，闫喜华被关押在双鸭山市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">晏萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女、广东省惠州市博罗县女教师、法轮功学员。原籍湖北省黄冈市麻城，后来户籍随夫迁往广东省惠州市博罗县罗阳镇，在罗阳镇第六小学任教，晏萍对待工作尽心尽力。因为坚持自己的信仰却屡遭迫害，从拘留到劳教，到进「洗脑班」，再到监狱，遭受了种种非人折磨，上「死人床」，多次被灌食，甚至被迫害致残，历经九死一生；最后公职亦被非法开除，医保、社保被全面停掉，维持生活的经济来源也被彻底截断。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年下半年，晏萍才出冤狱时，满头白发，经常头疼、头晕，无故出虚汗、大汗淋漓。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底，亲友联系晏萍时，发现她已失联多天。经多方打听，直到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，才得知她被关押在博罗县罗阳镇梅花看守所里。晏萍<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">燕宝萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：四川攀枝花市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生。原来是攀枝花机电学院校办会计，坚持信仰法轮大法，多次遭绑架、抄家，被开除工作；两次被非法劳教共四年，在四川资中楠木寺女子劳教所遭受到非人折磨。女儿被迫退学。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，燕宝萍在出租房内做法轮功资料时，被攀枝花市东区分局及临江路派出所警察抓捕。之后，燕宝萍被关押到盐边县看守所，后又被转入市看守所，现被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">燕秀红</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河北邢台市广宗县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，广宗县葫芦乡燕红龙村村民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，广宗县公安局国保带领武警闯入燕秀红的家中，企图抓捕燕秀红。燕秀红在争执中走脱。警察抄走燕秀红的法轮功书籍、现金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元、银行卡<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个、存折<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个和电脑、打印机等物品。燕秀红因此被迫流离失所。到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日燕秀红被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被构陷到法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月燕秀红被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/19/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8C%97%E9%82%A2%E5%8F%B0%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E7%87%95%E7%A7%80%E7%BA%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-431266.html"><span mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏银川市灵武市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US"> 1963</span>年生，是患有严重小儿麻痹后遗症的残疾人。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，严英修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被抓捕、关押构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被吴忠市利通区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。被迫害致乳腺癌、肝囊肿、胆结石，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月入到吴忠市医院。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/24/%E9%81%AD%E7%BB%91%E6%9E%B6%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4-%E5%AE%81%E5%A4%8F%E6%AE%8B%E7%96%BE%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%A5%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3%E8%87%B4%E7%99%8C%E7%97%87-433962.html</span></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨波：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，广东深圳南山、福田公安警察同时出动，非法抓捕了七位法轮功学员，分别是杨波、肖颖、豆君、朱薏、刘利军（音）、陈小燕与吴治明。其中：刘利军（音）被深圳福田公安抓捕，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天内获释。吴治明，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，被罗湖公安分局警察绑架并抄家，在罗湖看守所出现高血压，被关押<span lang="EN-US">39</span>天后回家。杨波，善良、热心，从小就乐于助人，也很有正义感。他太太肖颖是某国际知名外企深圳总公司的高管——财务部经理，据说学法轮功时间不长。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>时许，深圳市南山区高新派出所十几个警察（可能包括南山公安分局国保警察）到杨波、肖颖家敲门，警察用冲击钻钻坏两道铁门后，闯入杨波家，在没有出示立案通知书和搜查证的情况下非法抄家。抄走了法轮功书籍、电脑等等私人物品。期间一警察甚至掏出手抢，指向杨波恫吓，也不怕手枪走火。随后，杨波和肖颖夫妻俩被非法抓捕。杨波十三岁的女儿也被警察绑架到派出所几小时，孩子被警察讯问，最后孩子被亲属接回。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，杨波、肖颖、豆君被庭审，四名律师配合默契：三位律师侧重做信仰合法的无罪辩护，辩护很精彩。他们的辩护没被法官打断，但法官似乎心不在焉，没注意听。另一位律师强调办案人员的种种违法行径。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，广东省深圳市中级法院终审判决，维持深圳市南山区法院对上诉人杨波、肖颖定罪量刑的一审判决。杨波被以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金人民币一万元。其妻子肖颖被以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并处罚金人民币三千元。杨波刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨成云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。杨成云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杨大云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，江西九江市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年出生，江西省九江市德安县人，高中文化，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被抓，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年并处罚金一万。杨大云曾经<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被判刑一年劳教。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.yuanming.net/articles/a160640-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.yuanming.net/articles/a160640-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨德新</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，江西省宜春市万载县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，江西省万载县罗城镇横坑村人。一九九九年七月二十日中共发动对法轮功的疯狂迫害后，杨德新因坚持对法轮功信仰，遭受了十一年的冤狱迫害：<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在江西省豫章监狱，杨德新遭受了体罚、辱骂、毒打、悬空吊铐、长时间奴工劳动及强制精神洗脑等各种折磨。杨德新<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被抓捕，后一直被关押在南昌市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，南昌市第一看守所的在线上账软件显示，杨德新本人已不在看守所，显示「查无此人」。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，杨德新已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前可能被非法关押在南昌监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，家住青岛市崂山北宅。法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，曾被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，杨桂芳在城阳区集市被城阳区分局夏庄派出所抓捕抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，青岛即墨法院对杨桂芳开庭。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，青岛即墨法院当庭判刑杨桂芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月刑期，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">杨海霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">黑龙江省大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，杨海霞在家中被捕，关押到杜蒙县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，大庆市让胡路法院判杨海霞刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。杨海霞上诉到大庆市中级法院，九月中旬被枉法裁决：维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，杨海霞被送黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/24/2022-2-24.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁。一九九八年七月杨华修炼法轮大法后绝处逢生。杨华曾遭两年劳教迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在家被绑架、判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年（至今连判决书都没有看到），出狱回到家中不到三年时间再遭劫持，已被关押在汉台看守所近一年半；杨华、兀亚莉<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日讲法轮功真相时，被汉中市汉台区鑫源派出所警察绑架并非法抄家，被非法关押在汉台区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，兴汉新区公安分局警察分别告知家人她们已被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月上旬，杨华被汉中市汉台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨华明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：成都法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，在四川省妇幼保健院工作。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，成都市武侯区公安分局晋阳派出所警察和遂宁市射洪县青岗镇派出所警察在杨华明老家抓捕了他。杨华明在被关押期间，武侯区检察院以证据不足两次将材料退回晋阳派出所补充侦察，期间派出所警察和武侯区检察院警察利诱威逼杨华明及其家属：不认罪就重判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，杨华明被武侯区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨家敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省武汉市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被抓捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，武汉市法轮功学员杨家敏被构陷案，武汉市律师通知被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。现在杨家敏被关押在江岸看守所，因疫情，不转押，要家人送中药治疗，不让接见。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439420.html#22225224638-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/2/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439420.html#22225224638-2</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨建录：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省张家口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日下午，杨建录和妻子王惠君在建国街市场讲法轮功，被跟踪他们的宣化县公安分局国保大队警察绑架，家中物品被警察抄走。两天后，王惠君回家，杨建录一直被关押在宣化看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">二零二零年九月四日，杨建录被宣化区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河北省张家口市宣化法院对法轮功学员杨建录判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金一万元。杨建录家属正在上诉和控告。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨金德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日出生，河南省南阳市人，南阳市“奥奔”汽车销售有限责任公司（下称奥奔公司）实际控制人、董事长，民营企业家，中国国民党革命委员会（简称“民革党”）成员，南阳市第四届政协委员，前南阳市政法系统廉政监督员，企业维权上访者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月以来，因创办“奥奔”汽车销售有限责任公司（下称奥奔公司），随着企业绩效日益增高及销售规模不断扩大，其公司随很快成为河南省知名企业，其本人亦成为当地著名的民营企业家，被地方政府看重，并曾被委任为南阳市第四届政协委员和南阳市法院、检察院的廉政监督员；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾因一场经济纠纷，其公司集体财产被南阳市卧龙区法院划账私分，且法院院长滥用职权，暴力执法办案，随其公司员工先去银行抗议，继而又去法院投诉，但都毫无果效；其为捍卫员工合法权益，就带领员工连夜进京上访，然而，正是基于此次上访行为，最终导致其及公司众员工遭到的更大厄运；当其被一位南阳市卧龙区副区长带人从北京劝回后，其及公司上下相关员工<span lang="EN-US">22</span>人立即遭遇南阳市警方以“涉黑案”大抓捕；据悉，其被抓之初，曾被旋即送往一警犭基地关押审讯，期间，因长时间惨遭“吊大秤”、“与狼共舞”和“鬼洗脸”等<span lang="EN-US">15</span>种酷刑折磨，导致其身体严重伤残，瘫痪在看守所长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年之久；其眼耳手脚因多处受伤、断裂、损毁又不给予及时治疗，故而长期无法愈合，直至后来被准予会见新的代理律师时，其左眼视力已坏死，腿脚已萎缩，血压值极高；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月２日<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">23</span>人“涉黑案”在河南省南阳市唐河县法院开庭审理，并被一审以“组织、领导黑社会性质组织罪，聚众扰乱社会秩序罪，妨害作证罪，强迫交易罪，寻衅滋事罪，妨害公务罪”六项罪名分别宣判，其中，其被六罪并罚判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元；其他<span lang="EN-US">22</span>名被告人分别亦被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-10</span>年不等刑期或管制或单处罚金；其等<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人不服上诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，知其等多人案经南阳市中级法院二审裁决，虽有所减刑，但其仍被以“组织、领导黑社会性质组织罪，聚众扰乱社会秩序罪，妨害作证罪，强迫交易罪，妨害公务罪”５罪并罚，重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。目前在河南省第二监狱（河南省新乡市建设路<span lang="EN-US">64</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">453002</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨金凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南昌市西湖区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，万筱萍、杨金凤在永正外街，陈丽萍在站前西路锦峰大酒店门口被东湖公安分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，南昌市西湖区法院送达了对陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤及万金莲的刑事判决书，陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，万金莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。因<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均办理了「取保候审」，刑期均从判决执行之日起算。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨金霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省秦皇岛昌黎县武各庄法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，杨金霞在大夫庄集市上讲真相时，被人举报说发法轮功真相资料，遭三个便衣抓捕。在抓到马坨店派出所。后警察从其家中抄走法轮功书籍、周刊等私人物品。把她带到秦皇岛市公安医院，查出肺结核，肺气肿，当时随去的警察吓得都戴上了口罩。让杨金霞回家后开始监视居住，家门口总有蹲坑的，致使生活受到严重的干扰。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，昌黎法院判杨金霞<span lang="EN-US">,4</span>年徒刑，罚款五千元钱。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，重新收监。继续关押在河北女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">杨锦贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省海丰县乌坎维权村民，因乌坎事件而遭广东当局的疯狂报复，被广东当局定为“乌坎魏永汉、洪永忠等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人聚众扰乱社会秩序，非法集会、游行、示威，聚众扰乱交通秩序，妨害公务，故意传播虚假信息案”积极参加者，被控“未依照法律规定向主管机关提出申请而擅自举行集会、游行、示威，经政府主管机关告诫后，又拒不服从解散命令，严重破坏社会秩序”，属直接责任人员。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被当地警方刑拘，后转正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被广东省海丰县法院一审以“非法集会、游行、示威罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”等，共判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨靖波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">昆明法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功学员杨靖波、武存仙、倪会仙由于在小区粘贴「法轮大法好！真善忍好！」不干胶，和向住户赠送「天赐洪福」法轮功小册子，被安宁市金方街道办事处不法人员告发，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被安宁市国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被西山区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，杨靖波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨立才：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁籍艺术家、《零八宪章》签署者。杨立才是音像艺术家，曾在北京<span lang="EN-US">798</span>艺术区开设工作室和制品店。杨立才是《零八宪章》签署者，为了追求艺术自由及精神自由，于<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年左右从辽宁漂泊到北京，自创独立音乐场景工作室“白糖罐声场”，成为北京地区活跃的异见艺术家之一。自在法院宣判现场公开声援刘晓波、要求与刘晓波同罪事件后，杨立才受到严密监控。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日北京市第一中级法院宣判刘晓波“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”成立，判处刘晓波有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。刘晓波案宣判后，在法院外声援的杨立才接受采访后向现场的警察投案，要求陪刘晓波坐牢。杨立才后被押往八宝山派出所，做完笔录被限制数小时后于当晚获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初因发表涉港言论遭，杨立才被辽宁省盘锦市警方从深圳抓捕，其在深圳的租住屋遭到查抄，警方查押了他的电脑等物品。后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52182883"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨丽威：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52182883;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，邓玉林、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。杨丽威刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨丽霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。杨丽霞<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日往外挂法轮功挂件时，被南开区长虹派出所警察抓捕。警察又强行抄走家中电脑、打印机、塑封机、大法书籍多本、真相币上千元等其它众多私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日下午五点多钟，杨丽霞被 “取保候审” 放回家，被监视，不准上班。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日接到南开区派出所通知，对她的构陷案件已移交到天津市南开区检察院，在家等消息。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日八点半，杨丽霞在南开区法院被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨丽艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省松原市前郭县白依拉嘎乡红光农场村六分场屯法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被松原市公安局国保大队抓捕，丈夫陈海林（不炼功）也被抓捕，警察抄家，抢劫走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台笔记本计算机、师父法像、可能还有大法书籍、几部手机等私人物品。杨丽艳被关押在松原市善友看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨明玉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，山东省聊城地区临清巿人，上访维权人士，零八宪章签署者。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因发生工伤事故而遇不公，自此加入上访群体，也因此曾被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>次。由于在上访过程中屡遭不公与不幸，深感只有追求民主宪政才是唯一的出路，随毅然投入到推进中国民主宪政的事业中，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾多次积极参与举牌要求官员财产公示、呼吁公民基本权利等活动。以上行为最终招致当局的不满与忌恨，随于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被深圳市警方秘密拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被深圳巿警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其案在深圳市中级法院开庭审判；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，终被深圳市中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。一直被羁押于深圳市福田区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日刑满释放。杨明玉又于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪遭山东临清市警方刑事拘留。被关押在山东临清看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨秋仁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，广东省广州市天河区法院非法宣判，法轮功学员杨秋仁被判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。广州市天河区法轮功学员杨秋仁、杨金花，因为通过快递给天河区派出所警察邮寄法轮功学员无辜被迫害的真相资料，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被天河区警方以“破坏法律实施”为由，将两人关押到天河区看守所。杨秋仁今年（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年）<span lang="EN-US">4</span>岁，江西省丰城市杜市镇人，在广州从事装修方面的工作。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年，杨秋仁在广州第一军医大学炼功点开始修炼法轮功。他做事认真，老实厚道，性格很好。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，中共开始迫害法轮功后，杨秋仁去北京上访，被勒索了<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万多元。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年左右，因为讲述法轮功真相，杨秋仁在广州被绑架，冤判八年，后被劫入江西新建县监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年才结束冤狱回家。本次刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨秋雨：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京维权人士。杨秋雨先生，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日早晨在家中，遭到丰台区公安分局以<span lang="EN-US">“</span>涉嫌寻衅滋事罪<span lang="EN-US">”</span>抓捕，然而家属第二天拿到的拘留通知书上，落款日期居然是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，也就是说，丰台区公安分局在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年就决定在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年全国<span lang="EN-US">“</span>两会<span lang="EN-US">”</span>前夕，以<span lang="EN-US">“</span>寻衅滋事罪<span lang="EN-US">”</span>抓捕了杨秋雨，而丰台区检察院明知这是在制造冤假错案，仍然于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日批准了对杨秋雨先生的逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日才在丰台区法院正式开庭；据悉，看守所羁押期间，因上厕所曾遭警方虐待，被扣带<span lang="EN-US">18</span>斤脚镣长达半个月之久；其妻因被指控是与其案件相关的证人而被禁止参加旁听；至今未予宣判。目前被羁押于北京市丰台区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨荣丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，山西省霍州市人，基督徒，前山西师范大学老干部处公职人员，原山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会负责人、传道人，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年全职负责教会以来，将原本几十人的小教会发展成拥有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名基督徒的大型教会<span lang="EN-US">;2004</span>年，曾因在临汾市兴建金灯台大教堂而遭到当局的严厉打压（含断水断电等各种形式的阻挠）<span lang="EN-US">;2009</span>年，因当局看中该教会所在地商业价值，欲强拆金灯台教堂而被其坚决拒绝，随遭到临汾市浮山县政府的强烈报复，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，竟出动警察<span lang="EN-US">500</span>多名，围堵冲击教会会场和属于该教会的福音鞋厂，殴打致伤百余名基督徒<span lang="EN-US">; </span>后因双方就当地警方野蛮冲击打砸、围殴教会及基督徒的理赔事宜等在协商中发生异议，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日该教会再遭武警包围<span lang="EN-US">; </span>同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其与<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名教会领袖到太原市上访维权，而被警方在途中劫持<span lang="EN-US">; </span>同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被山西省临汾市警方以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">"</span>非法占用农用地罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>、<span lang="EN-US">"</span>聚众扰乱交通秩序罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑拘，关押于山西省太原拘留所<span lang="EN-US">; 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被山西省临汾市尧都区批准以涉嫌同罪名正式批捕<span lang="EN-US">;2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被山西省临汾市尧都区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，后送往山西省新康监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US">;2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其与另<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名教会神职人员及负责人、同工等突然又被临汾市尧都区警方莫名带走<span lang="EN-US">; 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。目前被羁押于山西省临汾市尧都区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_29.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_29.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨荣霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省石家庄市藁城区法轮功学员。男，家住石家庄市藁城区增村镇杨马村，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在家中被河北省保定市望都县警察和河北省公安厅警察抓捕。警察抄走两车私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年（具体月份不详），杨荣霞被藁城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现关押于唐山监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">杨雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">福建省宁德市霞浦县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、庄友布、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，杨雄被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。据悉，此前这<span lang="EN-US">9</span>名法轮功学员之中，杨雄因信法轮功曾被判刑，并与肖传雄一起关押在福建省龙岩监狱服刑，惨遭狱警残害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，杨雄被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杨绍政</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，四川省巴中市人，成都市温江区学府尚郡暂住居民，中国农工党党员，西南财经大学经济学博士，前重庆工商大学教师，原贵州大学经济学院教授、硕士生导师和贵州大学高等教育评估与研究专家，贵州大学经济类学科首个被引进人才，中国知名经济学者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年大学毕业参加工作后，又于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年起进入贵州大学任教，被该校视为经济类学科首个引进的人才以来，一直深得该校的好评和荣耀，然之后因其经常发表令中共当局敏感和忌讳的政治言论，随屡遭贵州当局的监控与维稳打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因网发揭露中共党政人员每年耗费<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万亿元人民币等的相关信息，而被贵州大学叫停授课，且此前就曾因涉政言论而两次被贵州省公安厅约谈和被明确警告在中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大期间“闭嘴”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被贵州大学以发表敏感言论为由正式开除；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“六四”期间，曾因其在微信群讲<span lang="EN-US">38</span>军军长徐勤先的司机披露说六四杀了<span lang="EN-US">3000-5000</span>名学生，随立刻被贵州省政法委、贵州省网信办及多名警察以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤；传唤中，遭虐待式审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多小时，双手被戴手铐、脚镣，和固定在老虎椅子上，并被要求其衣服脱光、抽血、采集十指指纹及尿检等；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年中共“十·一”期间，曾又遭贵州省政法委控制而软禁多日；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因杨绍政频发政治敏感言论，虽遭警方警告也不停息，遂再次被贵州省贵阳市花溪区警方秘密带走。自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，知其被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政府罪”指定居所监视居住。后杨绍政遭正式逮捕。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日杨绍政被贵阳市公安局侦查终结，以涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪移送贵阳市人民检察院审查起诉。辩护律师于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日会见了杨绍政教授。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，贵州省贵阳市人民检察院已经将杨绍政教授涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权案件起诉到贵阳市中级法院。杨绍政教授不认为自己有任何违法犯罪行为，杨绍政教授认为如果任由掌握公权的人不受制约的枉法滥权，每一个中国人都有可能受到自己所受到的可怕遭遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">此前杨绍政教授的辩护律师曾代理控告办案人员刑讯逼供、虐待被监管人，贵阳市人民检察院答复称控告不属实。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，辩护律师再次向贵州省人民检察院提起了相关办案人员涉嫌构成刑讯逼供罪、虐待被监管人罪的控告。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前杨绍政被关押在贵阳市乌当区三江农场第一看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_72.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_72.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_42.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;
